Open Ctrip map to filter for five-star and above hotels here. It is the only choice. There is a private garden in such a location. I personally think it is much higher than Lujiazui. It is a scene in itself.

Although the room layout is quite satisfactory, as a five-star hotel in Shanghai, it can be said that the quality is absolutely online with a large number of wood veneer decorations, comfortable bedding, Dyson hair dryers, Ferragamo supplies, Chinese welcome refreshments, etc.

To be honest, the breakfast is at a normal five-star level, but the East Lake Hall Chinese Restaurant should be of a very high standard (I regret not going to experience it). However, in such a location, who wouldn‚Äôt walk nearby and order a fried dish, a bowl of stewed wontons, or walk into a beautifully decorated bistro to have a leisurely brunch to complement today‚Äôs day? A wonderful start to citywalk?

The service is definitely the highlight. As an old state-owned hotel, the service of Donghu Hotel is far better than that of overseas luxury brands. The enthusiasm and thoughtfulness are just right. We were upgraded to a suite when we checked in, which was an absolute surprise.

Hotels with similar style in Shanghai include Ruijin InterContinental, Jianyeli Capella, and Wukang Road Mansion (Mahler Villa personally feels a bit rough, so I won't include them). Their geographical location is the best in East Lake, and their garden design is unparalleled among other hotels in InterContinental. On the right, Capella‚Äôs croquettes are full. I think the positioning of Wukang Road Mansion is a bit awkward. If you want to be in the center of "rich and prosperous", then Donghu Hotel is the best choice; if you care about "cost-effectiveness", Donghu Hotel's price of 1k on weekdays is already the biggest conscience (it will definitely be more expensive during holidays).

Overall, East Lake Hotel is definitely an excellent place to stay that I would recommend to my friends.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:City-view Room
info:Stayed in September 2023
info:Other
info:10 Reviews
rating:4
posted:Posted September 6, 2023
msg:This place was once called "Du Mansion", but Du Yuesheng himself fled to Hong Kong with his wife and concubines because of the outbreak of the "August 13" Sino-Japanese Battle of Songhu in Shanghai. He never lived here for even a day. After that, it was rented out and used as the U.S. Embassy in Shanghai. After the founding of the People's Republic of China, it was taken over by the Shanghai Municipal People's Government and renamed the East Lake Hotel. However, it was only used for internal government receptions and was opened to the public after the reform and opening up. It is currently affiliated with East Lake. A well-known five-star garden hotel under the group. Although the garden is not big, the small European-style fountain in the garden still makes people feel a sense of age; the lobby is luxuriously decorated, and the old-fashioned elevator is as old as ever. Although it is a bit small, it is in line with the characteristics of its own old hotel; the rooms are hard-decorated, The soft furnishings and old-style plumbing appliances in the bathroom are imaginable; the receptionist and housekeepers provide decent service and greet each other with a smile; but the breakfast buffet is priced at more than 100 yuan, which may be because there are too few guests for dining that day. Too much to say. Overall, it was a pleasant trip to a garden-style hotel.

3. It is not recommended to eat breakfast in the hotel. The dishes are too simple and there are only a few more items than ordinary business express hotels. Besides, except for the soup noodle section, everything else is cold food. Even the stir-fry at 7:40 is already cold. ;
4. There is a peculiar smell in the lobby, which seems to be due to the smell of rags or mops. Please pay more attention to the hygiene of cleaning supplies;
5. Of course, there are still advantages. The hotel has very good sound insulation. Although the room faces the road this time, the sound is instantly muted as soon as the window is closed.
All in all, I won't stay here again in the future.
